Google Drive â†’ ìƒë‹¨ **ìƒˆë¡œ ë§Œë“¤ê¸° > ë”ë³´ê¸° > Apps Script**  \n2. ì•„ë˜ ì½”ë“œë¥¼ ë¶™ì—¬ë„£ê¸°  \n3. `TARGET_FOLDER_ID`ì— ì •ë¦¬í•  í´ë” ID ì…ë ¥  \n   - í´ë” ì—´ê³  URLì˜ `folders/` ë’¤ ë¬¸ìì—´ì´ ID  \n4. ë¨¼ì € `DRY_RUN = true`ë¡œ **ë¯¸ë¦¬ë³´ê¸° ì‹¤í–‰** â†’ ë¡œê·¸ í™•ì¸  \n5. ë¬¸ì œ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ `DRY_RUN = false`ë¡œ ë°”ê¾¸ê³  ë‹¤ì‹œ ì‹¤í–‰\n\n```javascript\n/** ====== Drive íŒŒì¼ ìë™ íƒœê¹…/ì´ë¦„ë³€ê²½ v1 (DONALDìš©) ====== **/\n\nconst CONFIG = {\n  TARGET_FOLDER_ID: 'ì—¬ê¸°ì—_í´ë”ID_ì…ë ¥',   // ì˜ˆ: '1abcD...'\n  DRY_RUN: true,                            // trueë©´ ë¯¸ë¦¬ë³´ê¸°, falseë©´ ì‹¤ì œë³€ê²½\n  DATE_FROM_FILENAME_IF_ANY: true,          // íŒŒì¼ëª…ì— ë‚ ì§œê°€ ìˆìœ¼ë©´ ìš°ì„  ì‚¬ìš© (ì˜ˆ: 2024-11-12)\n  DEFAULT_DATE_FMT: 'yyyy-MM-dd'            // Utilities.formatDateì—ì„œ ì‚¬ìš©\n};\n\n// ê°„ë‹¨ í‚¤ì›Œë“œâ†’íƒœê·¸ ì‚¬ì „(í•„ìš”ì‹œ ì¶”ê°€/ìˆ˜ì •)\nconst DICT = {\n  company: {\n    'ì‚¼ì„±ì „ì': '#ì‚¼ì„±ì „ì', 'í˜„ëŒ€ì°¨': '#í˜„ëŒ€ì°¨',\n    'LGì—ë„ˆì§€ì†”ë£¨ì…˜': '#LGì—ë„ˆì§€ì†”ë£¨ì…˜', 'ì—”ë¹„ë””ì•„': '#ì—”ë¹„ë””ì•„'\n  },\n  sector: {\n    'ë°˜ë„ì²´': '#ë°˜ë„ì²´', '2ì°¨ì „ì§€': '#2ì°¨ì „ì§€', 'ìë™ì°¨': '#ìë™ì°¨', 'AI': '#AI'\n  },\n '#2023', '2024': '#2024', '2025': '#2025',\n    '1ë¶„ê¸°': '#1ë¶„ê¸°', '2ë¶„ê¸°': '#2ë¶„ê¸°', '3ë¶„ê¸°': '#3ë¶„ê¸°', '4ë¶„ê¸°': '#4ë¶„ê¸°'\n  }\n};\n\n// íŒŒì¼ëª…ì—ì„œ ë‚ ì§œ í¬ë§· ì¶”ì¶œ (YYYY-MM-DD, YYYY.MM.DD ë“±)\nfunction extractDate(name) {\n  const patterns = [\n    /(\\d{4})[-._](\\d{2})[-._](\\d{2})/, // 2024-11-12 or 2024.11.12\n    /(\\d{4})(\\d{2})(\\d{2})/            // 20241112\n  ];\n  for (const p of patterns) {\n    const m = name.match(p);\n    if (m) {\n      const y = m[1], mo = m[2], d = m[3];\n      return `${y}-${mo}-${d}`;\n    }\n  }\n  // ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì˜¤ëŠ˜\n  return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), CONFIG.DEFAULT_DATE_FMT);\n}\n\n// ê°„ë‹¨ í‚¤ì›Œë“œ ë§¤ì¹­\nfunction guessTags(name) {\n  const lower = name.toLowerCase();\n  const pick = (dict) => {\n    for (const k in dict) {\n      if (lower.includes(k.toLowerCase())) return dict[k];\n    }\n    return null;\n  };\n  const tags = [];\n  const c = pick(DICT.company); if (c) tags.push(c);\n  const s = pick(DICT.sector);  if (s) tags.push(s);\n  const t = pick(DICT.topic);   if (t) tags.push(t);\n  const ti = pick(DICT.time);   if (ti) tags.push(ti);\n  return [...new Set(tags)];\n}\n\nfunction buildNewName(file) {\n  const oldName = file.getName();\n  const ext = oldName.includes('.') ? '.' + oldName.split('.').pop() : '';\n  const base = ext ? oldName.slice(0, -ext.length) : oldName;\n\n  const dateStr = CONFIG.DATE_FROM_FILENAME_IF_ANY ? extractDate(base) :\n    Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), CONFIG.DEFAULT_DATE_FMT);\n\n  const tags = guessTags(base);\n  if (tags.length === 0) tags.push('#ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸');\n\n  const newBase = `[${dateStr}]_${tags.join('_')}_v1`;\n  return newBase + ext;\n}\n\nfunction renameInFolder() {\n  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.TARGET_FOLDER_ID);\n  const files = folder.getFiles();\n  let count = 0;\n\n  while (files.hasNext()) {\n    const f = files.next();\n    const oldName = f.getName();\n    const newName = buildNewName(f);\n\n    if (oldName === newName) {\n      Logger.log(`= ë™ì¼: ${oldName}`);\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    if (CONFIG.DRY_RUN) {\n      Logger.log(`ë¯¸ë¦¬ë³´ê¸°: \"${oldName}\" â†’ \"${newName}\"`);\n    } else {\n      f.setName(newName);\n      Logger.log(`ë³€ê²½ ì™„ë£Œ: \"${oldName}\" â†’ \"${newName}\"`);\n    }\n    count++;\n  }\n  Logger.log(`ì²˜ë¦¬ ê°œìˆ˜: ${count} (DRY_RUN=${CONFIG.DRY_RUN})`);\n}\n```\n\n**íŒ**  \n- íšŒì‚¬/ì—…ì¢…/ì£¼ì œ ì‚¬ì „(DICT)ì„ **ì—¬ëŸ¬ í‚¤ì›Œë“œ**ë¡œ ëŠ˜ë ¤ë‘ë©´ ì •í™•ë„ê°€ ì­‰ ì˜¬ë¼ê°‘ë‹ˆë‹¤.  \n- ì²˜ìŒì—” ìƒìœ„ 1~2ê°œ í´ë”ë¡œë§Œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸í•˜ì„¸ìš”.\n\n---\n\n# 2) ê³ ê¸‰ â€” Python ì¼ê´„ë³€ê²½ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ (ë¡œì»¬ì—ì„œ ì‹¤í–‰)\n\n> ì¥ì : ê·œì¹™ì„ ë” ì •êµí•˜ê²Œ ì»¤ìŠ¤í„°ë§ˆì´ì¦ˆ, ëŒ€ëŸ‰ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì‰¬ì›€  \n> ì „ì œ: Google Driveë¥¼ PCì— ë™ê¸°í™”í•˜ê±°ë‚˜, Drive API ìê²©ì„ ì„¤ì •\n\n## A. ì‚¬ìš© ìˆœì„œ\n1) í´ë” ê²½ë¡œ ì§€ì • â†’ 2) **DRY_RUN**ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¯¸ë¦¬ë³´ê¸° â†’ 3) OKë©´ ì‹¤ì œ ë³€ê²½\n\n```python\n# rename_invest_reports_v1.py\nimport os, re, datetime\nDRY_RUN = True\nROOT = r\"C:\\Users\\YOU\\Drive\\Investment_Research\"  # ë™ê¸°í™” í´ë” ê²½ë¡œ\n\nDICT = {\n    \"company\": {\"ì‚¼ì„±ì „ì\":\"#ì‚¼ì„±ì „ì\",\"í˜„ëŒ€ì°¨\":\"#í˜„ëŒ€ì°¨\",\"LGì—ë„ˆì§€ì†”ë£¨ì…˜\":\"#LGì—ë„ˆì§€ì†”ë£¨ì…˜\",\"ì—”ë¹„ë””ì•„\":\"#ì—”ë¹„ë””ì•„\"},\n    \"sector\": {\"ë°˜ë„ì²´\":\"#ë°˜ë„ì²´\",\"2ì°¨ì „ì§€\":\"#2ì°¨ì „ì§€\",\"ìë™ì°¨\":\"#ìë™ì°¨\",\"AI\":\"#AI\"},\n    \"topic\":  {\"ë°¸ë¥˜ì—ì´ì…˜\":\"#ë°¸ë¥˜ì—ì´ì…˜\",\"ì‹¤ì \":\"#ì‹¤ì \",\"ì„±ì¥ì„±\":\"#ì„±ì¥ì„±\",\"ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬\":\"#ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬\",\"ì „ëµ\":\"#ì „ëµ\",\"ì‚°ì—…\":\"#ì‚°ì—…ë¶„ì„\"},\n    \"time\":   {\"2023\":\"#2023\",\"2024\":\"#2024\",\"2025\":\"#2025\",\"1ë¶„ê¸°\":\"#1ë¶„ê¸°\",\"2ë¶„ê¸°\":\"#2ë¶„ê¸°\",\"3ë¶„ê¸°\":\"#3ë¶„ê¸°\",\"4ë¶„ê¸°\":\"#4ë¶„ê¸°\"},\n}\n\ndate_patterns = [\n    re.compile(r\"(\\d{4})[-._](\\d{2})[-._](\\d{2})\"), # 2024-11-12\n    re.compile(r\"(\\d{4})(\\d{2})(\\d{2})\")           # 20241112\n]\n\ndef extract_date(name):\n    for p in date_patterns:\n        m = p.search(name)\n        if m:\n            y, mo, d = m.groups()\n            return f\"{y}-{mo}-{d}\"\n    return datetime.date.today().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d\")\n\ndef pick_tag(name, mapping):\n    low = name.lower()\n    for k, v in mapping.items():\n        if k.lower() in low:\n            return v\n    return None\n\ndef suggest_new_name(path):\n    base = os.path.basename(path)\n    stem, ext = os.path.splitext(base)\n    date_str = extract_date(stem)\n    tags = []\n\n    for key in [\"company\",\"sector\",\"topic\",\"time\"]:\n        t = pick_tag(stem, DICT[key])\n        if t and t not in tags:\n            tags.append(t)\n\n    if not tags:\n        tags.append(\"#ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸\")\n\n    new_stem = f\"[{date_str}]_{'_'.join(tags)}_v1\"\n    return new_stem + ext\n\ndef walk_and_preview(root):\n    for dirpath, _, filenames in os.walk(root):\n        for fn in filenames:\n            old = os.path.join(dirpath, fn)\n            new = os.path.join(dirpath, suggest_new_name(old))\n            if old != new:\n                print((\"ë¯¸ë¦¬ë³´ê¸°: \" if DRY_RUN else \"ë³€ê²½: \") + f\"{old} -> {new}\")\n                if not DRY_RUN:\n                    try:\n                        os.rename(old, new)\n                    except Exception as e:\n                        print(\"ì—ëŸ¬:\", e)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    walk_and_preview(ROOT)\n```\n\n- ë¨¼ì € `DRY_RUN = True`ë¡œ ì‹¤í–‰í•´ì„œ ë°”ë€” ì´ë¦„ì„ í™•ì¸  \n- ê´œì°®ìœ¼ë©´ `DRY_RUN = False`ë¡œ ë°”ê¾¸ê³  ë‹¤ì‹œ ì‹¤í–‰\n\n---\n\n# 3) ì›Œí¬í”Œë¡œ ì œì•ˆ (ì‹¤ìˆ˜
